  139. The false advertising alone is enough to warrant a one star review for this product. Despite the labeling on the tube, this product contains absolutely no retinol, much less 2.5%. Not that most people would want a 2.5% retinol because that would likely be too much for even the least sensitive skin types. No matter what spin or lingo this company attempts to use to justify their false labeling, retinol and retinyl palmitate are not the same ingredient and do not have the same results on the skin. Both are very good skin care ingredients but retinol is a much more powerful anti-aging ingredient.<br /><br />This company's claims that natural is better are also misleading given that a skin care ingredient isn't good or bad because it's synthetic or &#34;natural&#34;. It's good or bad because research has either shown it to have positive or negative results on skin. And regardless of what this or any other company says about their products being &#34;natural&#34;, there's very little if anything natural about what these ingredients need to go through to transform them into a product that is pleasing to the consumer.<br /><br />The only positive for this product is that the company has wisely left out the irritating ingredients like witch hazel that are found in so many of their other products. So, if you want to support a company who false advertises, you can purchase this product and you'll end up using a fairly good moisturizer (albeit way overpriced for what it is). There are much cheaper and much more effective options out there. And if you are truly looking for an anti-aging moisturizer, consult your dermatologist.
  140. This is a very disappointing product. In fact, this moisturizer doesn't even contain retinol. It's made with retinyl palmitate, which is an ester of retinol. The palmitate part is a 16-carbon tail that greatly attenuates the penetration and absorption of retinol. My guess is that OZ Naturals simply doesn't have the technology to stabilize retinol, so they use this derivative of it. With real retinol product even at 0.5% (Skinceuticals Retinol 0.5), I still cannot tolerate daily use. (I use three times a week.) But with this product, I can just jump to daily use with no reaction at all. Some people may think this is good, if they don't understand retinol. But in reality, this just means that the retinyl palmitate is much inferior. If you want real results, use real retinol products, not this stuff!

  213. Good Things are happening to my Mature and Dry Skin and I am not the only one to notice this improvement. I have not used all the skin care products in the Oz Naturals skin-care line, but this one is my favorite so far. I think that it is important to note that Super Youth Moisturizer is dispensed from a tube; therefore, there is less chance of bacterial contamination.<br /><br />Although, this moisturizer has benefits for anti-bacterial, anti-inflammatory, and anti-irritant, my prime interests are the anti-oxidants, and the anti-aging properties.<br /><br />Even though Super Youth Moisturizer has ingredients to help heal, and soothe acne, to smooth and soften scars and to help to heal skin sores, my skin condition mainly deals with dryness, sun damage, and the inevitable aging process, so this is what my personal review will address.<br /><br />The three main ingredients that are printed on the Super Youth Moisturizer are 2.5 RETINOL MOISTURIZER, HYALURONIC ACID, and VITAMIN E.<br /><br />RETINOL is a derivative of vitamin A, the stronger counterpart is tretinoin, which is the active ingredient in Retin-A. If your skin is too sensitive to use Retin-A, retinol is an excellent alternative. The reason that skin responds to skin care products with retinol, is that vitamin A has a molecular structure that is tiny enough to get into the lower layers of skin, where it finds collagen and elastin. Retinol is proven to improve mottled pigmentation, fine lines and wrinkles, skin texture, skin tone and color, and skin's hydration levels.<br /><br />My dermatologist had given me a prescription of Tretinoin Cream at 0.05%. I used this faithfully every night for 9 months, and although there was no skin irritation for me, I was constantly peeling and shedding my skin. Finally, after nine months I stopped using the tretinoin cream, I was no longer willing to suffer this continual ugly shedding, as this was both more noticeable, and less attractive than my skin condition. However, usage of the Super Youth moisturizer, which does have retinol, did NOT irritate nor have I had any of the shredding or peeling associated with Retinol, and my face skin tone and color is noticeably brighter.<br /><br />The second ingredient on the front of Super Youth Moisturizer is HYALURONIC ACID (HA) - The loss of natural hyaluronic acid is one of the causes of Wrinkles. Since topical products with HA cannot penetrate to deeper layers, the moisturizing effects will only last a few days. Repeated use will maintain moisture levels in the skin, preventing skin dehydration. Hyaluronic acid is useful for reducing or removing wrinkles, which makes the skin look younger and promotes an even skin tone, making it look smooth and supple. HA holds up to 1,000 times its weight in water, it functions not only to deliver water to the skin, but also to hold it there.<br /><br />I already do use a Hyaluronic Acid serum, and I apply it right after my Vitamin C serum. I will continue to use my HA serum even though Super Youth contains this ingredient, since I have dry skin. I live in the dry desert area of the southwest, and I definitely need to maintain the moisture levels that this acrid climate continues to eradicate.<br /><br />Vitamin E is so important for everyone's skin, it does not matter what unique skin condition each one of us has, it is necessary for all skin types, as this has to do with your general skin health. Vitamin E - Neutralizes free radicals UVA, UVB, infrared radiation A, and replenishes skin's Lipids (giving structure to cell membranes). As an anti-aging benefit, Vitamin E is an antioxidant; it both increases firmness, and reduces wrinkles.<br /><br />My Results: I have not even been using Super Youth for a full month, and yet my skin is noticeably brighter, the fine lines around my eyes have diminished, and are not noticeable when I am expressionless. My `smile' lines are also less prominent, but the most conspicuous improvement has been in my cheeks and neck! My cheeks are visibly smoother, almost completely line/wrinkle free, they are plumper and less sunken. My neck is also smoother; the tiny vertical lines running down toward my collarbone seemed to have disappeared.<br /><br />For those who are new to skin-care, it can be overwhelming with all the different product usages and the sequence of applications, so I thought that I would provide a general guideline to eliminate confusion.<br /><br />1. Always, wash and cleanse first.<br /><br />2. It is better to have a designated washcloth just for your face, as wet towels can breed bacteria.<br /><br />3. Apply your toner immediately following patting your face dry. It only takes 60 seconds before moisture tends to leave your skin, and the toner helps to lock in this necessary moisture.<br /><br />4. Apply your Vitamin C serum first. This needs to soak through the skin to the inner layers, so nothing other than the toner should come first.<br /><br />5. Apply your other facial serums, I use Hyaluronic Acid serum next, this retains 1,000 times its weight in water and not only does HA deliver water to your skin, it also helps to retain moisture, preventing dehydration.<br /><br />6. Any type of facial oils should be applied right BEFORE your moisturizer, since oils will soak into the skin, and your moisturizer sits on the top layer, providing an effective barrier.<br /><br />7. Next apply your moisturizer, I recommend Super Youth by Oz Naturals; it is the best moisturizer that I have ever used.<br /><br />8. Sunscreen comes next, no matter whether or not your foundation make-up contains it or not.<br /><br />9. Your facial skin has now been prepped and now you can finish off with your normal cosmetic<br />routine.<br /><br />To summarize this review on Super Youth Moisturizer, from my experience this moisturizer helps to repair cell damage and accelerates cell growth, for a healthier and better-looking complexion.<br /><br />Disclosure: Moisturizer sent for an evaluation, without any obligation, the research and opinions are my own.

  318. Good Things are happening to my Mature and Dry Skin and I am not the only one to notice this improvement. I have not used all the skin care products in the Oz Naturals skin-care line, but this one is my favorite so far. I think that it is important to note that Super Youth Moisturizer is dispensed from a tube; therefore, there is less chance of bacterial contamination.<br /><br />Although, this moisturizer has benefits for anti-bacterial, anti-inflammatory, and anti-irritant, my prime interests are the anti-oxidants, and the anti-aging properties.<br /><br />Even though Super Youth Moisturizer has ingredients to help heal, and soothe acne, to smooth and soften scars and to help to heal skin sores, my skin condition mainly deals with dryness, sun damage, and the inevitable aging process, so this is what my personal review will address.<br /><br />The three main ingredients that are printed on the Super Youth Moisturizer are 2.5 RETINOL MOISTURIZER, HYALURONIC ACID, and VITAMIN E.<br /><br />RETINOL is a derivative of vitamin A, the stronger counterpart is tretinoin, which is the active ingredient in Retin-A. If your skin is too sensitive to use Retin-A, retinol is an excellent alternative. The reason that skin responds to skin care products with retinol, is that vitamin A has a molecular structure that is tiny enough to get into the lower layers of skin, where it finds collagen and elastin. Retinol is proven to improve mottled pigmentation, fine lines and wrinkles, skin texture, skin tone and color, and skin's hydration levels.<br /><br />My dermatologist had given me a prescription of Tretinoin Cream at 0.05%. I used this faithfully every night for 9 months, and although there was no skin irritation for me, I was constantly peeling and shedding my skin. Finally, after nine months I stopped using the tretinoin cream, I was no longer willing to suffer this continual ugly shedding, as this was both more noticeable, and less attractive than my skin condition. However, usage of the Super Youth moisturizer, which does have retinol, did NOT irritate nor have I had any of the shredding or peeling associated with Retinol, and my face skin tone and color is noticeably brighter.<br /><br />The second ingredient on the front of Super Youth Moisturizer is HYALURONIC ACID (HA) - The loss of natural hyaluronic acid is one of the causes of Wrinkles. Since topical products with HA cannot penetrate to deeper layers, the moisturizing effects will only last a few days. Repeated use will maintain moisture levels in the skin, preventing skin dehydration. Hyaluronic acid is useful for reducing or removing wrinkles, which makes the skin look younger and promotes an even skin tone, making it look smooth and supple. HA holds up to 1,000 times its weight in water, it functions not only to deliver water to the skin, but also to hold it there.<br /><br />I already do use a Hyaluronic Acid serum, and I apply it right after my Vitamin C serum. I will continue to use my HA serum even though Super Youth contains this ingredient, since I have dry skin. I live in the dry desert area of the southwest, and I definitely need to maintain the moisture levels that this acrid climate continues to eradicate.<br /><br />Vitamin E is so important for everyone's skin, it does not matter what unique skin condition each one of us has, it is necessary for all skin types, as this has to do with your general skin health. Vitamin E - Neutralizes free radicals UVA, UVB, infrared radiation A, and replenishes skin's Lipids (giving structure to cell membranes). As an anti-aging benefit, Vitamin E is an antioxidant; it both increases firmness, and reduces wrinkles.<br /><br />My Results: I have not even been using Super Youth for a full month, and yet my skin is noticeably brighter, the fine lines around my eyes have diminished, and are not noticeable when I am expressionless. My `smile' lines are also less prominent, but the most conspicuous improvement has been in my cheeks and neck! My cheeks are visibly smoother, almost completely line/wrinkle free, they are plumper and less sunken. My neck is also smoother; the tiny vertical lines running down toward my collarbone seemed to have disappeared.<br /><br />For those who are new to skin-care, it can be overwhelming with all the different product usages and the sequence of applications, so I thought that I would provide a general guideline to eliminate confusion.<br /><br />1. Always, wash and cleanse first.<br /><br />2. It is better to have a designated washcloth just for your face, as wet towels can breed bacteria.<br /><br />3. Apply your toner immediately following patting your face dry. It only takes 60 seconds before moisture tends to leave your skin, and the toner helps to lock in this necessary moisture.<br /><br />4. Apply your Vitamin C serum first. This needs to soak through the skin to the inner layers, so nothing other than the toner should come first.<br /><br />5. Apply your other facial serums, I use Hyaluronic Acid serum next, this retains 1,000 times its weight in water and not only does HA deliver water to your skin, it also helps to retain moisture, preventing dehydration.<br /><br />6. Any type of facial oils should be applied right BEFORE your moisturizer, since oils will soak into the skin, and your moisturizer sits on the top layer, providing an effective barrier.<br /><br />7. Next apply your moisturizer, I recommend Super Youth by Oz Naturals; it is the best moisturizer that I have ever used.<br /><br />8. Sunscreen comes next, no matter whether or not your foundation make-up contains it or not.<br /><br />9. Your facial skin has now been prepped and now you can finish off with your normal cosmetic<br />routine.<br /><br />To summarize this review on Super Youth Moisturizer, from my experience this moisturizer helps to repair cell damage and accelerates cell growth, for a healthier and better-looking complexion.<br /><br />Disclosure: I Received a free sample of the Moisturizer for an evaluation, and without any obligation. The research and opinions are my own., they are plumper and less sunken. My neck is also smoother; the tiny vertical lines running down toward my collarbone seemed to have disappeared. For those who are new to skin-care, it can be overwhelming with all the different product usages and the sequence of applications, so I thought that I would provide a general guideline to eliminate confusion. 1. Always, wash and cleanse first. 2. It is better to have a designated washcloth just for your face, as wet towels can breed bacteria. 3. Apply your toner immediately following patting your face dry. It only takes 60 seconds before moisture tends to leave your skin, and the toner helps to lock in this necessary moisture. 4. Apply your Vitamin C serum first. This needs to soak through the skin to the inner layers, so nothing other than the toner should come first. 5. Apply your other facial serums, I use Hyaluronic Acid serum next, this retains 1,000 times its weight in water and not only does HA deliver water to your skin, it also helps to retain moisture, preventing dehydration. 6. Any type of facial oils should be applied right BEFORE your moisturizer, since oils will soak into the skin, and your moisturizer sits on the top layer, providing an effective barrier. 7. Next apply your moisturizer, I recommend Super Youth by Oz Naturals; it is the best moisturizer that I have ever used. 8. Sunscreen comes next, no matter whether or not your foundation make-up contains it or not. 9. Your facial skin has now been prepped and now you can finish off with your normal cosmetic routine. To summarize this review on Super Youth Moisturizer, from my experience this moisturizer helps to repair cell damage and accelerates cell growth, for a healthier and better-looking complexion. According to my research:<br />• Retinol is a form of Vitamin A that is known for its effectiveness in treating acne and wrinkles and improving the appearance of sun-damaged skin.<br />• Hyaluronic acid helps the cells in your skin absorb and retain moisture. Hyaluronic acid (HA) is a biopolymer naturally occurring is the skin and other tissues. Babies have a high level of HA (hence that soft, supple skin!) and as we age, we have less and less (hence the appearance of fine lines and wrinkles!).<br />• Vitamin E has long been used and recommended for its antioxidant properties and providing protection against UV radiation and other free radicals. It is said to decrease skin roughness, length of facial lines, and wrinkle depth.<br /><br />OZ Naturals’ Super Youth 2.5% Retinol Moisturizer with Hyaluronic Acid and Vitamin E boasts itself as “a powerful cocktail of antioxidants with Vitamin A, to diminish fine lines and signs of premature aging.” Packaged in a flip cap tube, the moisturizer is 71% organic and made in the USA.   462. **EDITED after learning more about the product: Two people wrote to me to tell me that this product, Oz Naturals 2.5% Retinol Moisturizer, does not, in fact, contain Retinol, but instead contains a different type of vitamin A product called Retinyl Palmitate. At first I argued, \\"But it has 2.5% Retinol written right on the front of the tube!\\" However, I went ahead, turned the tube over, and looked through the list of ingredients as was written there. Sure enough, the word \\"Retinol\\" was no where to be found among the list of ingredients. However, half way down the list, I did find the ingredient \\"Retinyl Palmitate\\". So I did some research, and there is quite a bit of information about Retinyl Palmitate to be found on the internet. And one thing that I came across over and over is that Retinyl Palmitate is not the same thing as Retinol. It is an \\"ester\\", (a chemical compound), formed from the reaction of retinol and palmitic acid. To be able to use it, the body has to first convert it into retinoid acid, then retinaldehyde, and finally retinoid acid. It is about 20% less potent than retinol and you need to use a lot of it for it to be effective. Plus, it does not have the same exfoliating effects as retinol... I would encourage you to research this product--both Oz Naturals 2.5% Retinol (?) Moisturizer and the ingredient Retinyl Palmitate--to see if this is truly the kind of product you had in mind... Now to my original review--- For the past three years, I have been using a different retinol product which only contains 1% retinol, less than half the amount Oz Naturals 2.5% Retinol claims to have in it. However, it has done wonders for my skin, leaving it glowing, minimizing fine lines, etc. I was always getting compliments on my skin. And even though I had build up a tolerance for it, it would, at times, still make my face red while it was working, and sometimes my face would still even peel a bit. Still, it's done wonders for my skin. However, as I am now 53 years old, I decided to up the ante a bit and go for a product that had more retinol in it. So, after reading the Amazon reviews, I chose Oz Naturals 2.5% Retinol Moisturizer. I assumed because this product has 2.5% retinol in it, which is more than double the product I am currently using, that I would firstly experience some redness, stinging, etc. due the powerful strength of the retinol. I also assumed that it would make a more impressive difference in my skin, even better than the 1% retinol product I am using now. Well, I have to say that I am not impressed with the Oz Natural product at all. I have to say that I find it hard to believe that this actually contains 2.5% retinol as it claims to. I feel and see absolutely no effects from this product. No redness, tingling, stinging as one might expect. I see no glow, no improvement in my skin's appearance. Nothing. If anything, it leaves a dulling film on my face, and I actually think my skin looks worse, more dull and blah, rather than better. In my overall opinion, this product performs as well as any inexpensive drugstore moisturizing product would, but I feel it does absolutely nothing to actually improve the appearance of my skin. And as I previously said, if anything, I believe it has made my skin look bland, it's dulled the glow that my face did have, and it has actually has worsened the appearance of my skin instead of improved it. I will not be re-ordering this product. I plan to go back to my 1% retinol cream that I have been using, and I will stick with that until I can get a doctor's prescription for Retin-A.

  511. I was considering buying this product until i got suspicious and i found out (on their website) that this contains Retinyl Palmitate, NOT Retinol - although it deceptively claims 2.5% clinical strength \\"retinol cream\\". Retinyl Palmitate is not the same thing, and needs to be converted to Retinol then to Retnoic Acid to do its work on the skin - therefore, you need more Retinyl Palmitate compared to Retinol to get similar results. You can Google it for more detailed information on the differences.<br /><br />In either case, just know that even though it sounds like you're getting more and something stronger, it's not 2.5% Retinol that you're buying (generally more expensive). Seller is trying to pass off as if the two are the same or the terms can be used interchangeably - they are NOT the same. And it's deceptive to label it as being Retinol when it's Retinyl Palmitate.

I wanted to share my experience with using the OZ Naturals Retinol Moisturizer, as well as my mom's experience:<br /><br />I have used many retinol moisturizers before, and most have not given me any issues.
